

This folder contains the solutions and related files for Injured Android CTF challenges.

The file <span class="hljs-code">`jadx-gui-1.5.1-all.jar`</span> is too large for GitHub and has been uploaded to Google Drive.

Setup and Required Tools
Install a virtual Android device (e.g., Pixel 4, Android 11.0).
Enable developer mode (Settings &gt; About Phone &gt; Tap Build Number 7 times).
Install the InjuredAndroid app using ADB:
bash
Kodu kopyala
adb install C:\Users\YourUsername\Downloads\InjuredAndroid-1.0.12-release.apk
Launch the app and proceed with the following steps.
Flag 1: Package Listing
Objective: Find the app package and extract the APK file.

Steps:

Open Powershell or Terminal and run the following commands:
bash
Kodu kopyala
adb shell pm list packages
adb shell pm list packages | Select-String injured
adb shell pm path b3nac.injuredandroid
Extract the APK file:
bash
Kodu kopyala
adb pull /data/app/.../b3nac.injuredandroid-.../base.apk
Once the file is successfully downloaded, youâ€™ve solved Flag 1.
Flag 2: Activity Enumeration
Objective: Start a specific activity within the InjuredAndroid app.

Steps:

Run the following command in Powershell:
bash
Kodu kopyala
adb shell am start -n b3nac.injuredandroid/b3nac.injuredandroid.b25lActivity
This command launches the required activity, solving Flag 2.
Flag 3: Broadcast Receiver Test
Objective: Trigger a broadcast receiver to uncover the flag.

Steps:

Run the following command:
bash
Kodu kopyala
adb shell am start -n b3nac.injuredandroid/.TestBroadcastReceiver
This command triggers the broadcast receiver and solves Flag 3.
Flag 4: Decompile APK
Objective: Decompile the APK file and extract the necessary information.

Steps:

Open the previously downloaded base.apk file using Jadx GUI.
Explore the code structure to locate the flag, often stored as a string in a specific file.
Flag 5: SQL Injection
Objective: Exploit a SQL Injection vulnerability in the app to retrieve the flag.

Steps:

Locate the SQL Injection test button within the InjuredAndroid app.
Enter the following payload:
sql
Kodu kopyala
' OR '1'='1
Review the results to retrieve and record the flag. <span class="hljs-section">## Setup and Required Tools</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Install a virtual Android device (e.g., Pixel 4, Android 11.0).
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Enable developer mode (Settings &gt; About Phone &gt; Tap Build Number 7 times).
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Install the InjuredAndroid app using ADB:
  <span class="hljs-code">```bash
  adb install C:\Users\YourUsername\Downloads\InjuredAndroid-1.0.12-release.apk
</span></code></div></div></pre><ul><li>Launch the app and proceed with the following steps.</li></ul><hr><h2>Flag 1: Package Listing</h2><h3>Objective:</h3><p>Find the app package and extract the APK file.</p><h3>Steps:</h3><ol><li><p>Open Powershell or Terminal and run the following commands:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Kodu kopyala</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">adb shell pm list packages
adb shell pm list packages | Select-String injured
adb shell pm path b3nac.injuredandroid
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p>Extract the APK file:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Kodu kopyala</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">adb pull /data/app/.../b3nac.injuredandroid-.../base.apk
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><p>Once the file is successfully downloaded, youâ€™ve solved Flag 1.</p><hr><h2>Flag 2: Activity Enumeration</h2><h3>Objective:</h3><p>Start a specific activity within the InjuredAndroid app.</p><h3>Steps:</h3><ol><li>Run the following command in Powershell:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Kodu kopyala</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">adb shell am start -n b3nac.injuredandroid/b3nac.injuredandroid.b25lActivity
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><p>This command launches the required activity, solving Flag 2.</p><hr><h2>Flag 3: Broadcast Receiver Test</h2><h3>Objective:</h3><p>Trigger a broadcast receiver to uncover the flag.</p><h3>Steps:</h3><ol><li>Run the following command:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Kodu kopyala</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">adb shell am start -n b3nac.injuredandroid/.TestBroadcastReceiver
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><p>This command triggers the broadcast receiver and solves Flag 3.</p><hr><h2>Flag 4: Decompile APK</h2><h3>Objective:</h3><p>Decompile the APK file and extract the necessary information.</p><h3>Steps:</h3><ol><li>Open the previously downloaded <code>base.apk</code> file using <strong>Jadx GUI</strong>.</li><li>Explore the code structure to locate the flag, often stored as a string in a specific file.</li></ol><hr><h2>Flag 5: SQL Injection</h2><h3>Objective:</h3><p>Exploit a SQL Injection vulnerability in the app to retrieve the
